        <script>
            function open_login(event) {
                if (event) {
                    event.preventDefault();
                }
                if (typeof YitPaywall != 'undefined') {
                    YitPaywall.openLoginPopUp(YitPaywall.ApiRroutesConfig.Origin + YitPaywall.ApiRroutesConfig.login);
                }
            }
            if (typeof YitPaywall != 'undefined') {
                if (YitPaywall.getQueryVariable('paywall-popup-type') == 'login') {
                    open_login();
                }
            }
        </script>
